         <p><strong><span>The official developer documentation is at: <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fdocs.alfresco.com%2Fcommunity%2Fconcepts%2Fdev-for-developers.html" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Developer guide | Alfresco Documentation</a>&nbsp;</span></strong></p>
         <p style="min-height: 8pt; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</p>
         <p><a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwikitest.alfresco.com%2Fwiki%2FCategory%3AJavaScript_API" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">JavaScript API</a><a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwikitest.alfresco.com%2Fwiki%2FCategory%3ACookbook" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Cookbook</a><br>This page is the central page for examples for the <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwikitest.alfresco.com%2Fwiki%2FJavaScript_API_" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">JavaScript API</a>.&nbsp;&nbsp; Feel free to add your examples to this.&nbsp;</p>
         <p>Example scripts can be found in the <em>Company Home/Data Dictionary/Scripts</em> folder in a default Alfresco installation.</p>

             <li> <a class="jive-link-anchor-small" href="#jive_content_id_Find_all_XML_Forms_of_a_Specific_Type_and_Return_the_XML_content">Find all XML Forms of a Specific Type and Return the XML content</a> </li> 
             <li> <a class="jive-link-anchor-small" href="#jive_content_id_Create_and_Assign_a_New_Datalist_Item">Create and Assign a New Datalist Item</a> </li> 
            </ul></li>
          </ul>
         </div>

         <h2 id="jive_content_id_Create_Backup_of_a_Document">Create Backup of a Document</h2>
         <p>Creates a backup of a document as it is added to a space:</p>
         <pre class="language-javascript line-numbers"><code><span class="comment token">// find the backup folder - create if not already exists</span><br><span class="keyword token">var</span> backupFolder <span class="operator token">=</span> space<span class="punctuation token">.</span><span class="token function">childByNamePath</span><span class="punctuation token">(</span><span class="string token">'Backup'</span><span class="punctuation token">)</span><span class="punctuation token">;</span><br><span class="keyword token">if</span> <span class="punctuation token">(</span>backupFolder <span class="operator token">==</span> <span class="keyword token">null</span> <span class="operator token">&amp;&amp;</span> space<span class="punctuation token">.</span><span class="token function">hasPermission</span><span class="punctuation token">(</span><span class="string token">'CreateChildren'</span><span class="punctuation token">)</span><span class="punctuation token">)</span><br><span class="punctuation token">{</span><br>&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="comment token">// copy the doc into the backup folder</span><br>&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="keyword token">var</span> copy <span class="operator token">=</span> document<span class="punctuation token">.</span><span class="token function">copy</span><span class="punctuation token">(</span>backupFolder<span class="punctuation token">)</span><span class="punctuation token">;</span><br>&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="keyword token">if</span> <span class="punctuation token">(</span>copy <span class="operator token">!=</span> <span class="keyword token">null</span><span class="punctuation token">)</span><br>&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="punctuation token">}</span><br><span class="punctuation token">}</span><span class="line-numbers-rows"><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span></span></code></pre>

         <h2 id="jive_content_id_Return_Result_Value">Return Result Value</h2>
         <p>Returning a result value. This is useful for scripts that are processed using URLs via the <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwikitest.alfresco.com%2Fwiki%2FURL_Addressability%23Script_Command_Processor" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Script Command Servlet</a>, as the results are returned as the HTML response from the servlet:</p>
         <pre class="language-javascript line-numbers"><code><span class="keyword token">function</span> <span class="token function">result</span><span class="punctuation token">(</span><span class="punctuation token">)</span><br><span class="punctuation token">{</span><br>&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="keyword token">return</span> <span class="string token">'The name of my home space is: '</span> <span class="operator token">+</span> userhome<span class="punctuation token">.</span>name<span class="punctuation token">;</span><br><span class="punctuation token">}</span><br><span class="token function">result</span><span class="punctuation token">(</span><span class="punctuation token">)</span><span class="punctuation token">;</span><span class="line-numbers-rows"><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span></span></code></pre>
         <p style="min-height: 8pt; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</p>
         <p>The following solution will also return a value if placed at the end of a script:</p>
         <pre class="language-javascript line-numbers"><code><span class="comment token">// script here</span><br><span class="comment token">// ...</span><br><span class="keyword token">var</span> result <span class="operator token">=</span> <span class="string token">'some results...'</span><span class="punctuation token">;</span><br>result<span class="punctuation token">;</span><span class="line-numbers-rows"><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span></span></code></pre>
         <p style="min-height: 8pt; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</p>

         <h2 id="jive_content_id_Change_Mime_Type_of_a_Document">Change Mime Type of a Document</h2>

         <pre class="language-javascript line-numbers"><code><span class="keyword token">var</span> file <span class="operator token">=</span> userhome<span class="punctuation token">.</span><span class="token function">createFile</span><span class="punctuation token">(</span><span class="string token">'testfile.html'</span><span class="punctuation token">)</span><span class="punctuation token">;</span><br>file<span class="punctuation token">.</span>content <span class="operator token">=</span> <span class="string token">'some HTML here'</span><span class="punctuation token">;</span><br>file<span class="punctuation token">.</span>mimetype <span class="operator token">=</span> <span class="string token">'text/html'</span><span class="punctuation token">;</span><span class="line-numbers-rows"><span></span><span></span><span></span></span></code></pre>
         <p style="min-height: 8pt; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</p>
         <h2 id="jive_content_id_Create_Document_and_Transform_it">Create Document and Transform it</h2>
         <p>Creates document content and converts it to new formats using the transformation API:</p>
         <pre class="language-javascript line-numbers"><code><span class="comment token">// create a plain text doc and convert to PDF, generated file will be placed in same space as          <h2 id="jive_content_id_Execute_Freemarker_Template">Execute Freemarker Template</h2>
         <p>Executes a template from the repository against the current Document node:</p>
         <pre class="language-javascript line-numbers"><code><span class="keyword token">var</span> template <span class="operator token">=</span> companyhome<span class="punctuation token">.</span><span class="token function">childByNamePath</span><span class="punctuation token">(</span><span class="string token">'/Data Dictionary/Presentation Templates/doc_info.ftl'</span><span class="punctuation token">)</span><span class="punctuation token">;</span><br><span class="keyword token">if</span> <span class="punctuation token">(</span>template <span class="operator token">!=</span> <span class="keyword token">null</span><span class="punctuation token">)</span><br><span class="punctuation token">{</span><br>&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="keyword token">var</span> result <span class="operator token">=</span> document<span class="punctuation token">.</span><span class="token function">processTemplate</span><span class="punctuation token">(</span>template<span class="punctuation token">)</span><span class="punctuation token">;</span><br>&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="comment token">// output result to the console - could just as easily save the content into a new node...</span><br>&nbsp;&nbsp; logger<span class="punctuation token">.</span><span class="token function">log</span><span class="punctuation token">(</span>result<span class="punctuation token">)</span><span class="punctuation token">;</span><br><span class="punctuation token">}</span><br><span class="line-numbers-rows"><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span></span></code></pre>
         <p>Builds a FreeMarker template directly in the script, also builds up an argument list for the template. The result of the template is saved to a new node as the content:</p>
         <pre class="language-javascript line-numbers"><code><span class="keyword token">var</span> template <span class="operator token">=</span> '<span class="line-numbers-rows"><span></span></span></code></pre>

         <h2 id="jive_content_id_Use_AVM_API_to_Process_Webproject_Store">Use AVM API to Process Webproject Store</h2>
         <p>{{AVMWarning}}<br>Example using the AVM API to process a webproject store - the store name is passed as <em>store</em> on the url arguments:</p>
         <pre class="language-javascript line-numbers"><code><span class="keyword token">if</span> <span class="punctuation token">(</span>args<span class="punctuation token">[</span><span class="string token">'store'</span><span class="punctuation token">]</span> <span class="operator token">==</span> <span class="keyword token">null</span><span class="punctuation token">)</span><br><span class="punctuation token">{</span><br>&nbsp;&nbsp;          <h2 id="jive_content_id_Find_out_what_repository_Actions_are_available">Find out what repository Actions are available</h2>
         <pre class="language-javascript line-numbers"><code><span class="keyword token">function</span> <span class="token function">result</span><span class="punctuation token">(</span><span class="punctuation token">)</span><br><span class="punctuation token">{</span> <br>&nbsp;&nbsp; <span class="keyword token">return</span> <span class="punctuation token">(</span>actions<span class="punctuation token">.</span>registered<span class="punctuation token">)</span><span class="punctuation token">;</span> <br><span class="punctuation token">}</span> <br><span class="token function">result</span><span class="punctuation token">(</span><span class="punctuation token">)</span><span class="punctuation token">;</span><span class="line-numbers-rows"><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span><span></span></span></code></pre>

         <p>[transform-image, mail, copy-to-web-project, extract-metadata, counter, check-in, simple-workflow, script, transform, remove-features, specialise-type, import, add-features, link-category, blog-post, move, copy, check-out]</p>

         <h2 id="jive_content_id_Find_all_XML_Forms_of_a_Specific_Type_and_Return_the_XML_content">Find all XML Forms of a Specific Type and Return the XML content</h2>
         <p>You can use the <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=https%3A%2F%2Fdeveloper.mozilla.org%2Fen%2FCore_JavaScript_1.5_Guide%2FProcessing_XML_with_E4X" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">E4X </a> module of Javascript to parse XML.</p>

                <div class="jive-rendered-content">
                 <p>The "Obsolete" tag was automatically applied to content that hadn't been edited in a couple of years. If you don't think it applies, you should remove it. But before removing it, consider if the content is likely to be maintained in this space, or if it is better to point people to the official documentation.</p>
                 <p style="min-height: 8pt; padding: 0px;">&nbsp;</p>
                 <p>I think this cookbook is an example of the sort of content we want to have here, so I removed the tag.</p>
